  <script>_satellite["_runScript2"](function(event, target, Promise) {

window.at_res_all_debug = [];



// GA Variable Set w/ AT Response Token

document.addEventListener(adobe.target.event.REQUEST_SUCCEEDED, function(e) {  

    var tokens = e.detail.responseTokens;

	var mbox_name = e.detail.mbox;

    var ecid = _satellite.getVisitorId().getMarketingCloudVisitorID();

    window.at_evt_all = e;

    window.at_res_all = e.detail;

    window.at_res_all_debug.push(window.at_res_all);

    window.at_res_tokens = tokens;

  

    if (isEmpty(tokens)) { 

      return; 

    } 

  

    var uniqueTokens = distinct(tokens); 

    uniqueTokens.forEach(function(token) {      

      

          // GA Impression Track

          // new

          //window.dataLayer.push({

          var at_token = {

            "event" : "at_impression",

            "at_marketingCloudId" : ecid,

            "at_categoryAffinity" : token["profile.categoryAffinity"],

            "at_activityName" : token["activity.name"],

            "at_experienceName" : token["experience.name"],

            "at_parameterName" : token["profile.at_parameter"]

          }

          _satellite.track("push_at_token",{"mbox_name" : mbox_name, "at_token" : at_token});

          //})

          

          //for global-target-mbox

          if(mbox_name == (undefined || null)){

            mbox_name = "global-target-mbox";

            dataLayer.push(at_token)

          }

          



       // end of token process

      

    });

   

    _satellite.logger.warn("Target Response Token Returned !!!");

  

}); 



function isEmpty(val) { 

  return (val === undefined || val == null || val.length <= 0) ? true : false; 

} 



function key(obj) { 

   return Object.keys(obj) 

  .map(function(k) { return k + "" + obj[k]; }) 

  .join(""); 

} 



function distinct(arr) { 

  var result = arr.reduce(function(acc, e) { 

    acc[key(e)] = e; 

    return acc; 

  }, {}); 



  return Object.keys(result) 

  .map(function(k) { return result[k]; }); 

} 

});</script>

  <script>_satellite["_runScript3"](function(event, target, Promise) {

var category = _satellite.getVar('JV - ga4_dataset.product.category3');

var sessionStoragePDPView = sessionStorage.getItem('PDPView');



if(sessionStoragePDPView == null){

    var PDPview = {};

    PDPview[category] = 1;

    sessionStorage.setItem('PDPView', JSON.stringify(PDPview));

} else {

    var PDPview = JSON.parse(sessionStoragePDPView);

    if(PDPview[category] == null){

        PDPview[category] = 1;

        sessionStorage.setItem('PDPView', JSON.stringify(PDPview));

    } else {

        PDPview[category] = PDPview[category] + 1;

        sessionStorage.setItem('PDPView', JSON.stringify(PDPview));

    }

}



if(PDPview[category] > 2){

    //Adobe Track Event

    adobe.target.trackEvent({

        "mbox": "PDPPageView3 Event",

        "params":{

            "profile.PDPPageView3": "yes|"+category

        }

    });

}





});</script> <!-- /* moved to header component: <sly data-sly-include="body.skiptomaincontent.html"></sly> */ -->
